27 template<typename DataType_>
28 class RumpfFunctionalUnrolled<DataType_,
29 Trafo::Standard::Mapping<Geometry::ConformalMesh<Shape::Simplex<3>, 3, DataType_>>> :
30 public RumpfFunctionalBase<DataType_>
31 {
32 public:
34 typedef RumpfFunctionalBase<DataType_> BaseClass;
35
37 typedef DataType_ DataType;
39 typedef Shape::Simplex<3> ShapeType;
41 typedef Trafo::Standard::Mapping<Geometry::ConformalMesh<ShapeType, 3, DataType_>> TrafoType;
43 static constexpr int world_dim = TrafoType::world_dim;
45 static constexpr int shape_dim = ShapeType::dimension;
47 typedef typename Intern::TrafoFE<TrafoType>::Space TrafoSpace;
48
50 typedef Tiny::Matrix<DataType_, Shape::FaceTraits<ShapeType,0>::count, world_dim> Tx;
52 typedef Tiny::Vector<DataType_, Shape::FaceTraits<ShapeType,0>::count*world_dim> Tgradh;
53
55 typedef Tiny::Matrix<DataType_, shape_dim, world_dim> TgradR;
56
58 typedef typename TrafoType::template Evaluator<ShapeType, DataType>::Type TrafoEvaluator;
60 typedef typename TrafoSpace::template Evaluator<TrafoEvaluator>::Type SpaceEvaluator;
61
62 private:
64 const int _exponent_det;
66 const bool _compute_frobenius;
68 const bool _compute_cof;
70 const bool _compute_det;
71
72 public:
76 explicit RumpfFunctionalUnrolled(
77 const DataType fac_frobenius_,
78 const DataType fac_det_,
79 const DataType fac_cof_,
80 const DataType fac_reg_,
81 const int exponent_det_) :
82 BaseClass( fac_frobenius_,
83 fac_det_,
84 fac_det_*(Math::sqrt( Math::sqr(fac_reg_) + DataType(1) )*Math::pow( DataType(1) + Math::sqrt(Math::sqr(fac_reg_) + DataType(1)), DataType(exponent_det_))),
85 fac_cof_,
86 fac_reg_),
87 _exponent_det(exponent_det_),
88 _compute_frobenius( (fac_frobenius_ > DataType(0)) ),
89 _compute_cof( (fac_cof_ > 0) ),
90 _compute_det( (fac_det_ > 0) )
91 {
92 XASSERTM(exponent_det_ == 1 || exponent_det_ == 2,"exponent_det must be 1 or 2!");
93 }
94
100 static String name()
101 {
102 return "RumpfFunctionalUnrolled<"+ShapeType::name()+">";
103 }
104
108 String info() const
109 {
110 const Index pad_width(30);
111 return name() + ":" + BaseClass::info() + String("\nexponent_det").pad_back(pad_width, '.')
112 + String(": ") + stringify(_exponent_det);
113 }
114
118 void eval_fval_grad(DataType& fval, Tx& grad, const TgradR& DOXY(mat_tensor), const TrafoEvaluator& DOXY(trafo_eval), const SpaceEvaluator& DOXY(space_eval), const Tx& x, const DataType& h)
119 {
120 fval = DataType(0);
121 grad.format(DataType(0));
122
123 DataType fval_frobenius(0);
124 DataType fval_cof(0);
125 DataType fval_det(0);
126 DataType fval_rec_det(0);
127
128 if(_compute_frobenius)
129 {
130 fval_frobenius = this->_fac_frobenius*compute_frobenius_part(x,h);
131 add_grad_frobenius_part(grad, x, h);
132 }
133
134 if(_compute_cof)
135 {
136 fval_cof = this->_fac_cof*compute_cof_part(x,h);
137 add_grad_cof_part(grad, x, h);
138 }
139
140 if(_compute_det)
141 {
142 if(_exponent_det == 1)
143 {
144 fval_det = this->_fac_det*compute_det_1_part(x,h);
145 fval_rec_det = this->_fac_rec_det*compute_rec_det_1_part(x,h);
146 add_grad_det_1_part(grad, x, h);
147 add_grad_rec_det_1_part(grad, x, h);
148 }
149 else
150 {
151 fval_det = this->_fac_det*compute_det_2_part(x,h);
152 fval_rec_det = this->_fac_rec_det*compute_rec_det_2_part(x,h);
153 add_grad_det_2_part(grad, x, h);
154 add_grad_rec_det_2_part(grad, x, h);
155 }
156 }
157
158 fval = fval_frobenius + fval_cof + fval_det + fval_rec_det;
159
160 //std::cout << std::scientific;
161 //std::cout << std::setprecision(16);
162
163 //Tx grad_frobenius(DataType(0));
164 //Tx grad_cof(DataType(0));
165 //Tx grad_cof1(DataType(0));
166 //Tx grad_det(DataType(0));
167 //Tx grad_rec_det(DataType(0));
168
169 //add_grad_frobenius_part(grad_frobenius, x, h);
170 //add_grad_cof_part(grad_cof, x, h);
171 //add_grad_cof_part_1(grad_cof1, x, h);
172 //add_grad_det_1_part(grad_det, x, h);
173 //add_grad_rec_det_1_part(grad_rec_det, x, h);
174
175 //std::cout << "grad_frobenius"<< std::endl << grad_frobenius << std::endl;
176 //std::cout << "grad_cof"<< std::endl << grad_cof << std::endl;
177 //std::cout << "grad_cof1"<< std::endl << grad_cof1<< std::endl;
178 //std::cout << "grad_cof2"<< std::endl << grad_cof-grad_cof1<< std::endl;
179 //std::cout << "grad_det"<< std::endl << grad_det << std::endl;
180 //std::cout << "grad_rec_det"<< std::endl << grad_rec_det << std::endl;
181 //
182 //std::cout << "x = " << std::endl << x << std::endl;
183 //std::cout << "h = " << std::endl << h << std::endl;
184 //std::cout << "fval = " << stringify_fp_sci(fval) << ", "
185 //<< stringify_fp_sci(fval_frobenius)<< ", "
186 //<< stringify_fp_sci(fval_cof)<< ", "
187 //<< stringify_fp_sci(fval_det) << ", "
188 //<< stringify_fp_sci(fval_rec_det) << std::endl;
189
190 //std::cout << "local grad " << std::endl << grad << std::endl;
191 }
192
193 void eval_fval_cellwise(DataType& fval, const TgradR& DOXY(mat_tensor), const TrafoEvaluator& DOXY(trafo_eval), const SpaceEvaluator& DOXY(space_eval), const Tx& x, const DataType& h, DataType& fval_frobenius, DataType& fval_cof, DataType& fval_det)
194 {
195 fval = DataType(0);
196 fval_frobenius = DataType(0);
197 fval_cof = DataType(0);
198 fval_det = DataType(0);
199
200 if(_compute_frobenius)
201 {
202 fval_frobenius = this->_fac_frobenius*compute_frobenius_part(x,h);
203 }
204
205 if(_compute_cof)
206 {
207 fval_cof = this->_fac_cof*compute_cof_part(x,h);
208 }
209
210 if(_compute_det)
211 {
212 if(_exponent_det == 1)
213 {
214 fval_det = this->_fac_det*compute_det_1_part(x,h);
215 fval_det += this->_fac_rec_det*compute_rec_det_1_part(x,h);
216 }
217 else
218 {
219 fval_det = this->_fac_det*compute_det_2_part(x,h);
220 fval_det += this->_fac_rec_det*compute_rec_det_2_part(x,h);
221 }
222 }
223
224 fval = fval_frobenius + fval_cof + fval_det;
225
226 //std::cout << "fval = " << stringify_fp_sci(fval) << ", " << stringify_fp_sci(fval_frobenius)<< ", " << stringify_fp_sci(fval_det) << ", " << stringify_fp_sci(fval_rec_det) << std::endl;
227
228 }
229
234#if defined(FEAT_COMPILER_INTEL) && (FEAT_COMPILER_INTEL < 1600)
235 void add_grad_h_part(Tx& grad, const TgradR& DOXY(mat_tensor), const TrafoEvaluator& DOXY(trafo_eval), const SpaceEvaluator& DOXY(space_eval), const Tx& x, const DataType& h, const Tgradh& grad_h)
236#else
237 void NOINLINE add_grad_h_part(Tx& grad, const TgradR& DOXY(mat_tensor), const TrafoEvaluator& DOXY(trafo_eval), const SpaceEvaluator& DOXY(space_eval), const Tx& x, const DataType& h, const Tgradh& grad_h)
238#endif
239 {
240
241 DataType frobenius_der_h(0);
242 DataType cof_der_h(0);
243 DataType det_der_h(0);
244 DataType rec_det_der_h(0);
245
246 if(_compute_frobenius)
247 {
248 frobenius_der_h = this->_fac_frobenius*compute_frobenius_der_h_part(x,h);
249 }
250
251 if(_compute_cof)
252 {
253 cof_der_h = this->_fac_cof*compute_cof_der_h_part(x,h);
254 }
255
256 if(_compute_det)
257 {
258 if(_exponent_det == 1)
259 {
260 det_der_h = this->_fac_det * compute_det_1_der_h_part(x,h);
261 rec_det_der_h = this->_fac_rec_det * compute_rec_det_1_der_h_part(x,h);
262 }
263 else
264 {
265 det_der_h = this->_fac_det * compute_det_2_der_h_part(x,h);
266 rec_det_der_h = this->_fac_rec_det * compute_rec_det_2_der_h_part(x,h);
267 }
268
269 }
270
271 DataType der_h(frobenius_der_h + cof_der_h + det_der_h + rec_det_der_h);
272
273 //std::cout << "norm_der_h = " << stringify_fp_sci(this->_fac_frobenius*norm_der_h) << std::endl <<
274 // " det_der_h = " << stringify_fp_sci(this->_fac_det*det_der_h) << std::endl <<
275 // " rec_det_der_h = " << stringify_fp_sci(this->_fac_rec_det*rec_det_der_h) << std::endl;
276 //std::cout << "full_der_h " << stringify_fp_sci(der_h) << std::endl;
277
278 for(int i(0); i < Tx::m; ++i)
279 {
280 for(int d(0); d < Tx::n; ++d)
281 {
282 grad(i,d) += der_h*grad_h(i*Tx::n + d);
283 }
284 }
285 } // add_grad_h_part
286
287
292#if defined(FEAT_COMPILER_INTEL) && (FEAT_COMPILER_INTEL < 1600)
293 DataType compute_frobenius_part(const Tx& x, const DataType& h)
294#else
295 DataType NOINLINE compute_frobenius_part(const Tx& x, const DataType& h)
296#endif
297 {
298 DataType fval_frobenius_part(0);
299 fval_frobenius_part = Math::pow(DataType(6)*h*h-DataType(3)*Math::sqr(x(0,0))+DataType(2)*x(0,0)*x(1,0)+DataType(2)*x(0,0)*x(2,0)+DataType(2)*x(0,0)*x(3,0)-DataType(3)*Math::sqr(x(0,1))+DataType(2)*x(0,1)*x(1,1)+DataType(2)*x(0,1)*x(2,1)+DataType(2)*x(0,1)*x(3,1)-DataType(3)*Math::sqr(x(0,2))+DataType(2)*x(0,2)*x(1,2)+DataType(2)*x(0,2)*x(2,2)+DataType(2)*x(0,2)*x(3,2)-DataType(3)*Math::sqr(x(1,0))+DataType(2)*x(1,0)*x(2,0)+DataType(2)*x(1,0)*x(3,0)-DataType(3)*Math::sqr(x(1,1))+DataType(2)*x(1,1)*x(2,1)+DataType(2)*x(1,1)*x(3,1)-DataType(3)*Math::sqr(x(1,2))+DataType(2)*x(1,2)*x(2,2)+DataType(2)*x(1,2)*x(3,2)-DataType(3)*Math::sqr(x(2,0))+DataType(2)*x(2,0)*x(3,0)-DataType(3)*Math::sqr(x(2,1))+DataType(2)*x(2,1)*x(3,1)-DataType(3)*Math::sqr(x(2,2))+DataType(2)*x(2,2)*x(3,2)-DataType(3)*Math::sqr(x(3,0))-DataType(3)*Math::sqr(x(3,1))-DataType(3)*Math::sqr(x(3,2)),DataType(2))/(h*h*h*h)/DataType(4);
300 return fval_frobenius_part;
301 }
302
307#if defined(FEAT_COMPILER_INTEL) && (FEAT_COMPILER_INTEL < 1600)
308 DataType compute_cof_part(const Tx& x, const DataType& h)
309#else
310 DataType NOINLINE compute_cof_part(const Tx& x, const DataType& h)
311#endif
312 {
313 DataType fval_cof_part (0);
314 fval_cof_part = 540#if defined(FEAT_COMPILER_INTEL) && (FEAT_COMPILER_INTEL < 1600)
541 void add_grad_det_1_part(Tx& grad_det_1_part, const Tx& x, const DataType& h)
542#else
543 void NOINLINE add_grad_det_1_part(Tx& grad_det_1_part, const Tx& x, const DataType& h)
544#endif
545 {
546 grad_det_1_part(0,0) += -this->_fac_det*Math::sqrt(DataType(3))*Math::sqrt(DataType(6))*(x(1,1)*x(2,2)-x(1,1)*x(3,2)-x(1,2)*x(2,1)+x(1,2)*x(3,1)+x(2,1)*x(3,2)-x(2,2)*x(3,1))/(h*h*h)/DataType(3);
547
548 grad_det_1_part(0,1) += -this->_fac_det*Math::sqrt(DataType(3))*Math::sqrt(DataType(6))*(-x(1,0)*x(2,2)+x(1,0)*x(3,2)+x(1,2)*x(2,0)-x(1,2)*x(3,0)-x(2,0)*x(3,2)+x(2,2)*x(3,0))/(h*h*h)/DataType(3);
549
550 grad_det_1_part(0,2) += -this->_fac_det*Math::sqrt(DataType(3))*Math::sqrt(DataType(6))*(x(1,0)*x(2,1)-x(1,0)*x(3,1)-x(1,1)*x(2,0)+x(1,1)*x(3,0)+x(2,0)*x(3,1)-x(2,1)*x(3,0))/(h*h*h)/DataType(3);
551
552 grad_det_1_part(1,0) += -this->_fac_det*Math::sqrt(DataType(3))*Math::sqrt(DataType(6))*(-x(0,1)*x(2,2)+x(0,1)*x(3,2)+x(0,2)*x(2,1)-x(0,2)*x(3,1)-x(2,1)*x(3,2)+x(2,2)*x(3,1))/(h*h*h)/DataType(3);
553
554 grad_det_1_part(1,1) += -this->_fac_det*Math::sqrt(DataType(3))*Math::sqrt(DataType(6))*(x(0,0)*x(2,2)-x(0,0)*x(3,2)-x(0,2)*x(2,0)+x(0,2)*x(3,0)+x(2,0)*x(3,2)-x(2,2)*x(3,0))/(h*h*h)/DataType(3);
555
556 grad_det_1_part(1,2) += -this->_fac_det*Math::sqrt(DataType(3))*Math::sqrt(DataType(6))*(-x(0,0)*x(2,1)+x(0,0)*x(3,1)+x(0,1)*x(2,0)-x(0,1)*x(3,0)-x(2,0)*x(3,1)+x(2,1)*x(3,0))/(h*h*h)/DataType(3);
557
558 grad_det_1_part(2,0) += -this->_fac_det*Math::sqrt(DataType(3))*Math::sqrt(DataType(6))*(x(0,1)*x(1,2)-x(0,1)*x(3,2)-x(0,2)*x(1,1)+x(0,2)*x(3,1)+x(1,1)*x(3,2)-x(1,2)*x(3,1))/(h*h*h)/DataType(3);
559
